##########################################
#
#    MATTS databank version  3.12.2021
#
##########################################
#
#    F O R M A T   I N F O
#
#  (# symbol starts comment line)
#
#  Settings used to generate the bank  are specified in section SETTINGS (just below the format info)
#
#  Each atom type is described in separate entry (which begins with keyword ENTRY and has to 
#  be precided by an empty line).
#
#  Each of the entries has the following sections:
#
#  COMMENT
#
#    Comments to the entry
#
#  NOI
#
#    Number of instances of pseudoatoms used to compute mean values of multipole model parameters
#
#  ATOM DESCRIPTORS
#
#  Each line characterizes one of atoms used in type definition.
#    For example if bank entry characterizes carbon atom connected to
#    aliphatic sp2 C and sp2 N atoms and to any nitrogen atom. Then the entry
#    section contains three lines describing the central atom and
#    the sp2 atoms:
#
# #  central atom
#      C1    CONNECTED_TO  C2,N3,N        PLANARITY +  PLANAR_RING_WITH_PLANAR_ATOMS -      IN_3_MEMBER_RING * IN_4_MEMBER_RING *
# #  1-st neighbors
#      C2    CONNECTED_TO  C1,X,X         PLANARITY +  PLANAR_RING_WITH_PLANAR_ATOMS -      IN_3_MEMBER_RING * IN_4_MEMBER_RING *
#      N3    CONNECTED_TO  C1,X           PLANARITY +  PLANAR_RING_WITH_PLANAR_ATOMS -      IN_3_MEMBER_RING * IN_4_MEMBER_RING *
#
#    The line for 'any N' atom is skipped since the atom does not have its
#    own descriptors (except of chemical element) and such a line would not
#    provide any new information. While needless it is however OK to add
#    such a line.
#
#    The first line is for central atom. While not required, all the other
#    lines are grouped by topological distance to the first atom.
#
#    Line starts from atom label which is composed of symbol of chemical element
#    directly followed by (consecutive) atom number.
#
#    CONNECTED_TO characterizes atom connectivity and as a list of atoms connected
#    to the atom. The neighbours can be specified by:
#      - label
#      - chemical element symbol (if there is no separate descriptors line for
#        given neighbour)
#      - by element symbol preceded by ! which indicates that the neighbour is of
#        any element except of that indicated one
#      - X which indicates any element
#      - * which indicates any number of neighbours of any type including zero
#    In addition, the central atom can be specified by - meaning the central atom has no neighbours.
#
#    PLANARITY - defined for atoms which has at least 3 first neighbours, it can take one
#    of three possible values:
#      + atom and its 1-st neighbours lay in one plane
#      - atom and its 1-st neighbours do not lay in one plane
#      * any or undefined planarity
#
#    PLANAR_RING_WITH_PLANAR_ATOMS - list of planar rings the atom belongs to sorted with ring size
#     e.g. 6A,5B,5. Characters are used to label the rings (this labelling allows to indicate if
#    atoms belong to the same or to different rings). It is also possible to specify rings without
#    labeling them by specifying their size only. If atom does not belong to
#    any ring it is indicated with '-' character, and with '*' if ring membership
#    is not defined. '+' means the atom belongs to any planar ring (one or more).
#    Setting used for perception of planar rings include the following:
#    ring planarity threshold
#    atom in ring planarity threshold
#    atom in planar ring max number of neighbours
#
#
#
#  LOCAL COORDINATE SYSTEM
#
#    XD style local coordinate system: ax1 p1 ax2 p2 R/L
#    ax1 and ax2 defines axis (X or Y or Z)
#    p1 and p2 defines direction, each can be specified in of the following ways:
#    - atom label (e.g. C1) - direction from central atom to point located at atom (C1)
#    - atom_symbol (atom_label) (e.g. N(C1)) - direction from central atom to point located at atom of element given by atom_symbol
#       bonded to atom specified in brackets (in the example any nitrogen atom connected to atom C1)
#    - r(ring label) (e.g. r(6A)) - direction from central atom to point in the centre of ring (6A)
#    - average_direction(atom_label_1,..,atom_label_n) (e.g. average_direction(C1,C2)) - average direction from
#      central atom to atom on the list (also element symbols instead of atom label can be used e.g. average_direction(N,N)) will be
#      an average direction of vector from central atom to two nitrogen atoms which are connected to the central atom)
#    - any_atom(atom_label) - direction from central atom to any atom bonded to atom specified with atom_label
#    - !chemical_element_symbol(atom_label)  - direction from central atom to any atom of different chemical element
#      than given by chemical_element_symbol bonded to atom specified with atom_label (e.g. !H(C1) - any non-hydrogen bonded to C1)
#    - any_orthogonal - any orthogonal to the other direction
#
#
#  SYMMETRY
#
#    Symmetry of the atomic electron density.
#
#  CHIRALITY
#
#    Three first-neighbours defining the handedness of the group is given.
#
#  MULTIPOLE MODEL PARAMETERS
#
#    (...)
#
#####################
#
# based on UBDB2018
# Kumar P, Gruza B, Bojarowski SA, Dominiak PM
#ACTA CRYSTALLOGRAPHICA SECTION A 75, 398-408, Published: FEB 2019
#[DOI: 10.1107/S2053273319000482]
#
#####################

SETTINGS
  covalent bond threshold 0.4
  atom planarity threshold 0.1
  ring planarity threshold 0.1
  atom in ring planarity threshold 0.1
  atom in planar ring max number of neighbours 3
  min plm 0.002
  n sigma 1.0
  minimal number of type instances 2

######################
#
#  H Y D R O G E N
#
######################
######################

ENTRY
